(************************************************************************

 Every fibration gives rise to an indexed category

 In this file, we prove that every fibration gives rise to an indexed
 category. This construction makes use of the fiber of a displayed
 category. The pseudofunctoriality of the fiber follows from the fact
 that we have a cleaving. Note that all relevant constructions for this
 file are already given in the directory on displayed categories, and
 here, they are only collected. Compared to that directory, the only new
 thing is that we prove the laws of indexed categories.

 Contents
 1. The data
 2. The laws
 3. The identitor and compositor are natural isos
 4. The indexed category from a fibration

 ************************************************************************)

Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.
[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Categories.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Isos.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Univalence.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Functors.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.NaturalTransformations.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.OppositeCategory.Core.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.DisplayedCats.Core.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.DisplayedCats.Isos.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.DisplayedCats.Fibrations.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.DisplayedCats.Fiber.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.DisplayedCats.Univalence.
Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.IndexedCategories.IndexedCategory.

Section FibrationToIndexedCat.
  Context {C : category}
          (D : disp_univalent_category C)
          (HD : cleaving D).

  (**
   1. The data
   *)
  
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
indexed_cat_data (C ^opp)

  
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
indexed_cat_data (C ^opp)

    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
C ^opp → univalent_category
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ x y : C ^opp,
(C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat → (?F₀ x ⟶ ?F₀ y)%cat
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ x : C ^opp,
(functor_identity (?F₀ x) ⟹ ?F₁ x x (identity x))%cat
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (x y z : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(g : (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat),
(?F₁ x y f ∙ ?F₁ y z g ⟹ ?F₁ x z (f · g))%cat

    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
C ^opp → univalent_category
 exact (λ x, univalent_fiber_category D x).
    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ x y : C ^opp,
(C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
→ ((λ x0 : C ^opp, univalent_fiber_category D x0) x
   ⟶ (λ x0 : C ^opp, univalent_fiber_category D x0) y)%cat
 exact (λ x y f, fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f).
    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ x : C ^opp,
(functor_identity
   ((λ x0 : C ^opp, univalent_fiber_category D x0) x)
 ⟹ (λ (x0 y : C ^opp) (f : C ^opp ⟦ x0, y ⟧),
    fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f) x x
     (identity x))%cat
 exact (λ x, fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity HD x).
    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (x y z : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(g : (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat),
((λ (x0 y0 : C ^opp) (f0 : C ^opp ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧),
  fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f0) x y f
 ∙ (λ (x0 y0 : C ^opp) (f0 : C ^opp ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧),
    fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f0) y z g
 ⟹ (λ (x0 y0 : C ^opp) (f0 : C ^opp ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧),
    fiber_functor_from_cleaving D HD f0) x z (f · g))%cat
 exact (λ x y z f g, fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp HD f g).
  Defined.

  (**
   2. The laws
   *)
  
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
indexed_cat_laws cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data

  
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
indexed_cat_laws cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data

    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (x y : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(xx : cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x),
identity ((cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f) xx) =
(# (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f)
   (indexed_cat_id cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x xx)
 · indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data
     (identity x) f xx
 · idtoiso
     (maponpaths
        (λ g : C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧,
         (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ g) xx)
        (id_left f)))%cat
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (x y : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(xx : cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x),
identity ((cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f) xx) =
(indexed_cat_id cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data y
   ((cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f) xx)
 · indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data f
     (identity y) xx
 · idtoiso
     (maponpaths
        (λ g : C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧,
         (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ g) xx)
        (id_right f)))%cat
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (w x y z : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ w, x ⟧)%cat)
(g : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(h : (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat)
(ww : cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data w),
(indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data g h
   ((cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f) ww)
 · indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data f
     (g · h) ww
 · idtoiso
     (maponpaths
        (λ k : C ^opp ⟦ w, z ⟧,
         (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ k) ww)
        (assoc f g h)))%cat =
(# (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ h)
   (indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data f g
      ww)
 · indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data
     (f · g) h ww)%cat

    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (x y : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(xx : cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x),
identity ((cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f) xx) =
(# (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f)
   (indexed_cat_id cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x xx)
 · indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data
     (identity x) f xx
 · idtoiso
     (maponpaths
        (λ g : C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧,
         (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ g) xx)
        (id_left f)))%cat
 
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
id_disp (HD x y f xx) =
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) (HD x y f xx))
  (id_right (identity y))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (HD x y f xx)
        (HD x y (f · identity x)%cat xx))
     (id_right (identity y))
     (cartesian_factorisation
        (HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx))
        (identity y)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (HD x y f xx)
              (HD x x (identity x) xx))
           (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
           (HD x y f xx ;; cartesian_factorisation
                             (HD x x (identity x) xx)
                             (identity x)
                             (transportb
                                (λ z : (C ⟦ x, x ⟧)%cat,
                                 xx -->[ z] xx)
                                (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
                                   x) (id_disp xx)))) ;; 
      cartesian_factorisation
        (HD x y (f · identity x)%cat xx) (identity y)
        (transportb
           (λ z : (C ⟦ y, x ⟧)%cat,
            HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) -->[
            z] xx)
           (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
              (identity x) f)
           (HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) ;; HD x
                                                 x
                                                 (identity
                                                 x) xx))) ;; 
   idtoiso
     (maponpaths (λ g : (C ⟦ y, x ⟧)%cat, HD x y g xx)
        ((pr212 C) y x f)))%mor_disp

xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
(id_disp (HD x y f xx) ;; HD x y f xx)%mor_disp =
(transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) (HD x y f xx))
   (id_right (identity y))

                                  xx -->[ z] xx)
                                 (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
                                    x) (id_disp xx)))) ;; 
       cartesian_factorisation
         (HD x y (f · identity x)%cat xx) (identity y)

            (λ z : (C ⟦ y, x ⟧)%cat,
             HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) -->[
             z] xx)
            (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
               (identity x) f)
            (HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) ;; 
             HD x x (identity x) xx))) ;; idtoiso
                                            (maponpaths
                                               (λ 
                                                g : 
                                                 (C
                                                 ⟦ y,
                                                 x ⟧)%cat,
                                                HD x y
                                                 g xx)
                                               ((pr212 C)
                                                 y x f))) ;; 
 HD x y f xx)%mor_disp

      
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
(id_disp (HD x y f xx) ;; HD x y f xx)%mor_disp =
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
  (cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f
     (id_right (identity y)))
  (transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity y · identity y · identity y)%cat
        (identity y · identity y)%cat f
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y)
           (identity y) (id_right (identity y))))
     (cartesian_factorisation
        (HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx))
        (identity y)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (HD x y f xx)
              (HD x x (identity x) xx))
           (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
           (HD x y f xx ;; cartesian_factorisation
                             (HD x x (identity x) xx)
                             (identity x)
                             (transportb
                                (λ z : (C ⟦ x, x ⟧)%cat,
                                 xx -->[ z] xx)
                                (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
                                   x) (id_disp xx)))) ;; 
      cartesian_factorisation
        (HD x y (f · identity x)%cat xx) (identity y)
        (transportb
           (λ z : (C ⟦ y, x ⟧)%cat,
            HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) -->[
            z] xx)
           (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
              (identity x) f)
           (HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) ;; HD x
                                                 x
                                                 (identity
                                                 x) xx)) ;; 
      idtoiso
        (maponpaths
           (λ g : (C ⟦ y, x ⟧)%cat, HD x y g xx)
           ((pr212 C) y x f)) ;; HD x y f xx)%mor_disp)

x, y: C ^opp

xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x

     (transportb
        (λ z : (C ⟦ y, x ⟧)%cat,

        (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
           (identity x) f)
        (HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) ;; HD x x

                                                 x) xx)) ;;

D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
  (maponpaths (compose (identity y))
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          (identity x) f) @
   assoc (identity y) (identity y)
     (f · identity x)%cat @
   maponpaths (compose (identity y · identity y)%cat)
     ((pr212 C) y x f @ ! id_left f) @
   assoc (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y · identity y)%cat
     (identity y · identity y)%cat f
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y)
        (identity y) (id_right (identity y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f
     (id_right (identity y)))
  (transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
     (! assoc (identity y) f (identity x))
     (cartesian_factorisation
        (HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx))
        (identity y)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (HD x y f xx)
              (HD x x (identity x) xx))
           (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
           (HD x y f xx ;; cartesian_factorisation
                             (HD x x (identity x) xx)
                             (identity x)
                             (transportf
                                (λ z : (C ⟦ x, x ⟧)%cat,
                                 xx -->[ z] xx)
                                (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
                                     x) (id_disp xx)))) ;; 
      HD x y f (HD x x (identity x) xx) ;; HD x x
                                             (identity
                                                x) xx)%mor_disp) =
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx) (! id_left f)
  (HD x y f xx)

! id_right f @
maponpaths (compose f)
  (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
       x) @
assoc f (identity x) (identity x) @
cancel_postcomposition (f · identity x)%cat
  (identity y · f)%cat (identity x)
  (id_right f @ ! id_left f) @
! assoc (identity y) f (identity x) @
maponpaths (compose (identity y))
  (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
       (identity x) f) @
assoc (identity y) (identity y) (f · identity x)%cat @
maponpaths (compose (identity y · identity y)%cat)
  ((pr212 C) y x f @ ! id_left f) @
assoc (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f @
cancel_postcomposition
  (identity y · identity y · identity y)%cat
  (identity y · identity y)%cat f
  (cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y)
     (identity y) (id_right (identity y))) @
cancel_postcomposition (identity y · identity y)%cat
  (identity y) f (id_right (identity y)) = ! id_left f

      apply homset_property.
    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (x y : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(xx : cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x),
identity ((cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f) xx) =
(indexed_cat_id cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data y
   ((cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ f) xx)
 · indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data f
     (identity y) xx
 · idtoiso
     (maponpaths
        (λ g : C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧,
         (cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data $ g) xx)
        (id_right f)))%cat
 
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
id_disp (HD x y f xx) =
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) (HD x y f xx))
  (id_right (identity y))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (HD x y f xx)
        (HD x y (identity y · f)%cat xx))
     (id_right (identity y))
     (cartesian_factorisation
        (HD y y (identity y) (HD x y f xx))
        (identity y)
        (transportb
           (λ z : (C ⟦ y, y ⟧)%cat,
            HD x y f xx -->[ z] HD x y f xx)
           (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
              y) (id_disp (HD x y f xx))) ;; cartesian_factorisation
                                               (HD x y
                                                 (identity
                                                 y · f)%cat
                                                 xx)
                                               (identity
                                                 y)
                                               (transportb
                                                 (λ 
                                                 z : 
                                                 (C
                                                 ⟦ y,
                                                 x ⟧)%cat,
                                                 HD y
                                                 y
                                                 (identity
                                                 y)
                                                 (HD x
                                                 y f
                                                 xx) -->[
                                                 z] xx)
                                                 (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
                                                 f
                                                 (identity
                                                 y))
                                                 (HD y
                                                 y

                                                 xx)) ;; 
      HD x y (identity y · f)%cat xx)%mor_disp) =
transportb (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx) (id_left f)
  (HD x y f xx)

HD: cleaving D
x, y: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
  (maponpaths (compose (identity y · identity y)%cat)
     ((pr112 C) y x f @ ! id_left f) @
   assoc (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y · identity y)%cat
     (identity y · identity y)%cat f
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y)
        (identity y) (id_right (identity y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f
     (id_right (identity y)))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (HD y y (identity y) (HD x y f xx)) (identity y)
     (transportb
        (λ z : (C ⟦ y, y ⟧)%cat,
         HD x y f xx -->[ z] HD x y f xx)
        (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
           y) (id_disp (HD x y f xx))) ;; cartesian_factorisation
                                            (HD x y
                                               (identity
                                                 y · f)%cat
                                               xx)
                                            (identity
                                               y)

                                               (λ

                                                 y)
                                                 (HD x
                                                 y f
                                                 xx) -->[

                                                 f
                                                 (identity
                                                 y))
                                               (HD y y
                                                 (identity
                                                 y)
                                                 (HD x
                                                 y f
                                                 xx) ;; 
                                                HD x y
                                                 f xx)) ;;

   maponpaths (compose (identity y · identity y)%cat)
     ((pr112 C) y x f @ ! id_left f) @
   assoc (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y · identity y)%cat
     (identity y · identity y)%cat f
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y)
        (identity y) (id_right (identity y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity y · identity y)%cat (identity y) f
     (id_right (identity y)))
  (transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
     (! id_left f) (HD x y f xx)) =
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx) (! id_left f)
  (HD x y f xx)

                                                 x f

   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · (identity z · identity z))%cat
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (h · (g · f))%cat
     (assoc (identity z) (identity z) (identity z)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
        (identity z) (id_right (identity z)) @
      id_right (identity z)))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (HD x z (h · g)%cat (HD w x f ww)) (identity z)
     (transportb
        (λ z0 : (C ⟦ z, x ⟧)%cat,
         HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) -->[
         z0] HD w x f ww)
        (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
           g h)
        (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; HD x y g
                                                (HD w
                                                 x f
                                                 ww))) ;; 
   (cartesian_factorisation
      (HD w z (h · g · f)%cat ww) (identity z)
      (transportb
         (λ z0 : (C ⟦ z, w ⟧)%cat,
          HD x z (h · g)%cat (HD w x f ww) -->[ z0] ww)
         (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
            f (h · g)%cat)
         (HD x z (h · g)%cat (HD w x f ww) ;; HD w x f
                                                ww)) ;; 
    (idtoiso
       (maponpaths
          (λ k : (C ⟦ z, w ⟧)%cat, HD w z k ww)
          ((pr222 C) z y x w h g f)) ;; HD w z
                                          (h · (g · f))%cat
                                          ww)))%mor_disp =

     (h · (g · f))%cat (id_right (identity z)))
  (cartesian_factorisation

           (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; HD x
                                                 y g
                                                 (HD w
                                                 x f
                                                 ww))) ;; 
      HD x z (h · g)%cat (HD w x f ww) ;; HD w x f ww)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww))) ww)
  (cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
     (h · (g · f))%cat (id_right (identity z)))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (HD y z h (HD w y (g · f)%cat ww)) (identity z)
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)))
           (HD w y (g · f)%cat ww))
        (id_right h @ ! id_left h)
        (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; cartesian_factorisation
                                                (HD w
                                                 y
                                                 (g
                                                 · f)%cat
                                                 ww)
                                                (identity
                                                 y)

                                                 f g)

                                                 y g

                                                 x f
                                                 ww) ;; 
                                                 HD w
                                                 x f
                                                 ww)))) ;;

     (HD w z (h · (g · f))%cat ww) (identity z)

        (λ z0 : (C ⟦ z, w ⟧)%cat,
         HD y z h (HD w y (g · f)%cat ww) -->[ z0] ww)
        (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
             (g · f)%cat h)
        (HD y z h (HD w y (g · f)%cat ww) ;; HD w y
                                               (g · f)%cat
                                               ww)) ;; 
   HD w z (h · (g · f))%cat ww)%mor_disp

     (assoc (identity z) (identity z) (identity z)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
        (identity z) (id_right (identity z)) @
      id_right (identity z)))
  (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; HD x y g
                                          (HD w x f ww) ;; 
   HD w x f ww)%mor_disp

                                                (HD w
                                                 x f
                                                 ww) -->[
                                              z] ww)
                                             (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
                                                 f g)
                                             (HD x y g
                                                (HD w
                                                 x f
                                                 ww) ;; 
                                              HD w x f
                                                ww))%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww))) ww)
  (assoc h g f @
   cancel_postcomposition (h · g)%cat
     (identity z · (h · g))%cat f
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          g h) @
   ! assoc (identity z) (h · g)%cat f @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          f (h · g)%cat) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (maponpaths (compose (identity z))
        ((pr222 C) z y x w h g f @
         ! id_left (h · (g · f))%cat)) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (assoc (identity z) (identity z)
        (h · (g · f))%cat) @
   assoc (identity z) (identity z · identity z)%cat
     (h · (g · f))%cat @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · (identity z · identity z))%cat
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (h · (g · f))%cat
     (assoc (identity z) (identity z) (identity z)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
        (identity z) (id_right (identity z)) @
      id_right (identity z)))
  (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; (HD x y g
                                           (HD w x f
                                              ww) ;; 
                                         HD w x f ww))%mor_disp

      
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ w, x ⟧)%cat
g: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
h: (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat
ww: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data w
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww))) ww)
  (cancel_postcomposition (h · identity y)%cat
     (identity z · h)%cat (g · f)%cat
     (id_right h @ ! id_left h) @
   ! assoc (identity z) h (g · f)%cat @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          (g · f)%cat h) @
   assoc (identity z) (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
     (h · (g · f))%cat (id_right (identity z)))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww))) ww)
     (assoc h (identity y) (g · f)%cat)
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)))
           ww)
        (maponpaths (compose h)
           (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
                f g))
        (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; (HD x y
                                                 g
                                                 (HD w
                                                 x f
                                                 ww) ;; 
                                               HD w x
                                                 f ww))%mor_disp)) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww))) ww)
  (assoc h g f @
   cancel_postcomposition (h · g)%cat
     (identity z · (h · g))%cat f
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          g h) @
   ! assoc (identity z) (h · g)%cat f @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          f (h · g)%cat) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (maponpaths (compose (identity z))
        ((pr222 C) z y x w h g f @
         ! id_left (h · (g · f))%cat)) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (assoc (identity z) (identity z)
        (h · (g · f))%cat) @
   assoc (identity z) (identity z · identity z)%cat
     (h · (g · f))%cat @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · (identity z · identity z))%cat
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (h · (g · f))%cat
     (assoc (identity z) (identity z) (identity z)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
        (identity z) (id_right (identity z)) @
      id_right (identity z)))
  (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; (HD x y g
                                           (HD w x f
                                              ww) ;; 
                                         HD w x f ww))%mor_disp

      
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ w, x ⟧)%cat
g: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
h: (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat
ww: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data w
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww))) ww)
  (maponpaths (compose h)
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          f g) @
   assoc h (identity y) (g · f)%cat @
   cancel_postcomposition (h · identity y)%cat
     (identity z · h)%cat (g · f)%cat
     (id_right h @ ! id_left h) @
   ! assoc (identity z) h (g · f)%cat @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          (g · f)%cat h) @
   assoc (identity z) (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
     (h · (g · f))%cat (id_right (identity z)))
  (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; (HD x y g
                                           (HD w x f
                                              ww) ;; 
                                         HD w x f ww))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww))) ww)
  (assoc h g f @
   cancel_postcomposition (h · g)%cat
     (identity z · (h · g))%cat f
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          g h) @
   ! assoc (identity z) (h · g)%cat f @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
          f (h · g)%cat) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (maponpaths (compose (identity z))
        ((pr222 C) z y x w h g f @
         ! id_left (h · (g · f))%cat)) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     (assoc (identity z) (identity z)
        (h · (g · f))%cat) @
   assoc (identity z) (identity z · identity z)%cat
     (h · (g · f))%cat @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · (identity z · identity z))%cat
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (h · (g · f))%cat
     (assoc (identity z) (identity z) (identity z)) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
     (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
        (identity z) (id_right (identity z)) @
      id_right (identity z)))
  (HD y z h (HD x y g (HD w x f ww)) ;; (HD x y g
                                           (HD w x f
                                              ww) ;; 
                                         HD w x f ww))%mor_disp

      
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
w, x, y, z: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ w, x ⟧)%cat
g: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
h: (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat
ww: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data w
maponpaths (compose h)
  (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof f
       g) @
assoc h (identity y) (g · f)%cat @
cancel_postcomposition (h · identity y)%cat
  (identity z · h)%cat (g · f)%cat
  (id_right h @ ! id_left h) @
! assoc (identity z) h (g · f)%cat @
maponpaths (compose (identity z))
  (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
       (g · f)%cat h) @
assoc (identity z) (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat @
cancel_postcomposition (identity z · identity z)%cat
  (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat
  (id_right (identity z)) =
assoc h g f @
cancel_postcomposition (h · g)%cat
  (identity z · (h · g))%cat f
  (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof g
       h) @
! assoc (identity z) (h · g)%cat f @
maponpaths (compose (identity z))
  (! fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof f
       (h · g)%cat) @
maponpaths (compose (identity z))
  (maponpaths (compose (identity z))
     ((pr222 C) z y x w h g f @
      ! id_left (h · (g · f))%cat)) @
maponpaths (compose (identity z))
  (assoc (identity z) (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat) @
assoc (identity z) (identity z · identity z)%cat
  (h · (g · f))%cat @
cancel_postcomposition
  (identity z · (identity z · identity z))%cat
  (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
  (h · (g · f))%cat
  (assoc (identity z) (identity z) (identity z)) @
cancel_postcomposition
  (identity z · identity z · identity z)%cat
  (identity z) (h · (g · f))%cat
  (cancel_postcomposition
     (identity z · identity z)%cat (identity z)
     (identity z) (id_right (identity z)) @
   id_right (identity z))

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

  (**
   3. The identitor and compositor are natural isos

  (indexed_cat_id cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x xx)

(g : (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat)

  (indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data f g
     xx)

  (indexed_cat_id cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x xx)
 
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
x: C ^opp
xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
is_z_isomorphism
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD x x (identity x) xx)
     (identity x)
     (transportb
        (λ z : (C ⟦ x, x ⟧)%cat, xx -->[ z] xx)
        (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity_data_subproof
           x) (id_disp xx)))

      apply is_nat_z_iso_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_identity.
    
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
∏ (x y z : C ^opp) (f : (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat)
(g : (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat)
(xx : cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x),
is_z_isomorphism
  (indexed_cat_comp cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data f g
     xx)
 
C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
x, y, z: C ^opp
f: (C ^opp ⟦ x, y ⟧)%cat
g: (C ^opp ⟦ y, z ⟧)%cat
xx: cleaving_to_indexed_cat_data x
is_z_isomorphism
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD x z (g · f)%cat xx)
     (identity z)
     (transportb
        (λ z0 : (C ⟦ z, x ⟧)%cat,
         HD y z g (HD x y f xx) -->[ z0] xx)
        (fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp_data_subproof
           f g)
        (HD y z g (HD x y f xx) ;; HD x y f xx)%mor_disp))

      apply is_nat_z_iso_fiber_functor_from_cleaving_comp.
  Defined.
